# 565 — The one window's presentation kernel: single-authority content, composition, run-structure (grounded-answer · run-render · navigation · the workflow/memory folds)

> **Long-form summary (the prior 5755-char frontmatter `title:`, moved into the body 2026-06-11 — it exceeded the indexer's title-metadata limit and broke indexing of this file; see observations.md):**
>
> 565 — The one window's CONTENT tier (shipped) + COMPOSITION tier (§12 — shipped): one grounded-answer authority, one run-status authority, one answer-presentation authority — and the render-composition that makes the answer LEAD (the content analog of 561's surface unification — 561 made two WINDOWS unrepresentable; 565 makes a grounded answer with no evidence projection, and a second grounded-answer authority, unrepresentable; the agent path is today an IMPOVERISHED FORK of the RAG path's grounding/status/answer chains, and the correct structure SUBSUMES the fork so verifiable local-passage citations, semantic status, and a single ordered run render are true in every mode by construction) + SPATIAL-COMPOSITION tier (§13 — SHIPPED 2026-06-05, live-validated): the run as a whole-conversation, prominence-graded status-spine + a GENERATED-zone composition — the principled refinement of 559 §8's deliberate deferral of layout composition (projected-content composition becomes governable by GENERATION, while bespoke-leaf composition stays hand-authored) + LEAF tier (§15 — SHIPPED 2026-06-06: §15.A–D via §15.H + the §15.J enforcement closure): the prior tiers unified the run TRUNK (record / tool-card / projection / spatial frame) but the LEAVES of the one concept 'a grounded claim rendered in a run' are still FORKED — the grounding scorer (3–4 sites, 2 threshold sets), the inline-citation weave (StreamingTextBlock vs MarkdownBlock), the answer text-renderer (plain vs markdown), and the workflow run (a bespoke WorkflowView, a 561 SECOND interaction surface) — because trunk-unification does not propagate to a leaf unless a typed authority-seam reaches it or a register positively covers it, and neither did; the correct structure completes the propagation (one grounding-semantics authority extending 559's Evidence seam, one answer-presentation + inline-citation weave, one run-render that workflow ADOPTS) and the anti-drift teeth are the typed Evidence seam (preferred over the grep gate) + the ALREADY-BUILT 561 interaction-surface gate, whose one-line fix is to bring `core.workflow-run` into its core-shape scope so the workflow fork becomes a build failure (§15.G de-risk corrected the earlier 'owed/unbuilt' claim) — no new kernel + RUN-STEP-PRESENTATION authority (§16 research / §17 design, 2026-06-09): the run status-spine's bare-dot/no-glyph nodes are one leaf of a FORKED run-step presentation — §3.B projects the tone facet, but glyph/label/prominence/bundle are hand-authored across ≥5 step-render sites (spine / in-body trace / tool-card / drawer / presence), 559's 'kernel half-applied to presentation' disease at the run-step element; the correct structure is ONE projected StepPresentation {tone, glyph, label, prominence, liveness} every step-surface composes through ONE run-node primitive — extending 559's engine + §3.B + Display's ICON facet + composeToolLabel + prominenceFor — seam(tier-2)+register-gate locked so a hand-rolled step presentation is unrepresentable (§17 SHIPPED + ④/⑤ grounding-honesty badge SHIPPED §18) + DENSITY-ADAPTIVE tier (§19, 2026-06-09 — design theory → SHIPPED §19.H, live measured-audit-verified; residuals + cross-tier ledger in §19.I): a live look showed the shipped run-step glyph is ILLEGIBLE at the spine-gutter scale — §17 unified the step's SEMANTICS but not the SCALE of its rendering; the correct structure is density-adaptive representation, the unbuilt FILL half of 559's Adaptivity authority (an element declares a representation ladder minimal→compact→full and the engine projects the legible one for the measured size, so an illegible-at-scale glyph is unrepresentable), the prominence grading projected from a declared (size,contrast) scale, the check-adaptive-closure gate extended to density — no new kernel; meta-principle: a SEMANTIC unification is incomplete until the rendering is legible at every SCALE it appears + NAVIGATION authority (§21 — SHIPPED chat-first 2026-06-10, live-validated + independently reviewed + merged; general multi-surface authority deferred to the 2nd adopter): every agent-window navigation issue this session (lopsided dots needing a hand-tuned balance-blend, the click-jump highlight the scroll-spy kept stealing, the chunky scrollbar beside the minimap, the rail that wouldn't collapse, 'make the spine the scrollbar') is ONE symptom — the run's spatial reading-and-navigation model is hand-wired in one view as FOUR forked representations (native scrollbar · viewport box · dots · active ring) bound by no authority; the correct structure is the sibling-to-Adaptivity NAVIGATION authority that 559 NAMED-BUT-NEVER-DESIGNED (it capped Adaptivity at element-level overflow/fill/placement) and 569/561 deferred: one canonical NavigableRun (the already-canonical ordered landmarks + per-landmark scroll-EXTENT + reading-WINDOW + DERIVED focus + a single live/pinned navigation INTENT) projected to every scroll surface via POSITION/WINDOW/FOCUS/CONTROL/AFFORDANCE facets — the minimap COMPOSES Adaptivity's placement+density + scrollViewport + composeGridStyles, the native scrollbar is TRANSPORT-not-authoring (the 559 §15 consumer-boundary ceiling), anti-drift is a navigation-surfaces register+gate (catalog/coverage/forbidden-reintroduction) over the typed NavigableRun seam — which re-seats the §13/§19 spine + §13.9 layout + the scrollbar as its FIRST projections and makes the balance-blend / highlight-pin / redundant-scrollbar / phantom-zone patches unrepresentable by construction; meta-principle: a run is not navigable until ONE authority owns where-each-event-is, where-you-are, and how-you-move, so the scroll affordance / minimap / position-box / focus-ring become projections, not four mechanisms that happen to agree


## §0 Purpose & scope

**In scope.** The *content* the one window (561) renders in its working state: the run, the tool calls, the approval moment, the reasoning, the answer, and — the layer we lack at parity — the **grounded evidence** behind the answer. Centred on the **agent** mode because it is the densest working state, but the authorities generalise to Documents / Structured / free chat. This doc designs the correct *content-authority* structure, not a styling pass.

**Out of scope.** The **information architecture** — one window, mode affordances, posture, the retrospective drawer — is 561's gate-locked result and is not revisited. The underlying **data records** (`Hit`, `ExcerptRegion`, `SearchTrace`, `ContextCitation`) are reused, not re-modelled. The proven **kernel** and the **existing presentation gates** are extended, never forked.

**Register.** Design theory in the project kernel (single authority → governed projection → register/gate). Feasibility and effort deliberately disregarded; major re-seats are in scope; end-states are stated at the bar the category now sets (NotebookLM-grade verifiable grounding; the agentic-tool semantic-status + collapsed-run grammar).

## §1 The corrected diagnosis — the agent path is an impoverished fork of the RAG path

A three-front investigation (presentation authorities; the grounding flow; the concrete components) found that the one window renders **two content lineages behind one frame**, because the agent path and the RAG path evolved separately. For each of three concepts there are two-or-three authorities, neither subordinate:

**Grounded answer.** RAG has the *full chain*: `ContextCitation` → `StreamingCitationMatcher` (matches answer spans back to sources) → a scored `CitationsPanel` with a working **local-file deep-link** (`citation-select` → `Shell.onCitationSelect` → `highlightCitation` / `openExternal`). The **agent** has the *data* at the tool boundary (`buildSearchEvidence` → `structuredData.searchResults` carries path/line/snippet) but: it renders **unscored, display-only** cards (`searchEvidence.renderSearchEvidence`) with **no deep-link**; `SearchTool.formatResults` flattens the hits to *prose* for the LLM; and the answer event **`AgentDone.finalResponse` is a bare string** — no citations, no source ids, no correlation. The RAG `StreamingCitationMatcher` has **no agent analog**. So the agent answer is grounded in fact but *carries no evidence the user can see or verify*. `CitationsPanel` is mounted **only in `SummarizeView`**, never the one window; `CitationHoverCard` (inline `[n]`) re-derives **its own** strong/moderate/weak scorer. → **No single grounded-answer authority; the agent is the impoverished fork.**

**Run status.** Three partial colour schemes for one concept: the retrospective drawer's History colours by `success` (green/red), its Timeline by `originator` (purple/teal), and the inline `ToolCallCard` tints its *border* by `risk` (danger/warning) while leaving the status text **colourless**. The drawer and the inline card even read **different models** (`ctrl.history[].success` vs `ToolCall.status`). And `AgentProgress.severity` (`INFO`/`WARN`/`ERROR`) is plumbed end-to-end but **unused at the renderer**. → **No single status authority; three partial schemes + a model split + a dangling severity.**

**Answer presentation.** The *same logical answer* renders as **markdown** (`jf-markdown-block`) in agent mode but **plain text** (`jf-streaming-text-block`) in chat/RAG mode; there is **no reading-width cap** (max-width is a container %, not a `ch` measure). And progress markers (the `conversation` array) and the streaming answer (a separate trailing `streamingText` block) render from **two different structures**, so the run has **no single ordered timeline** — the answer always renders last regardless of when its phase markers fired (the "markers below the answer" defect). → **Two answer renderers + no measure + a two-structure timeline.**

**What already exists and is reusable (the spine).** `evidenceProjection.ts` (`EvidenceItem`/`EvidenceScore`/`evidenceTier`/`filenameOf`) is a real single-authority projection. Semantic status tokens exist (`--accent-success/warning/danger` + alpha grades, theme-aware) and a `tone→token` projector exists (`SystemNotice`/`severityToTone`) — but scoped to *notices*, not lifecycle status. The right-drawer `OverlayHost` slot already stacks three drawers, and `RetrospectivePanel` proves the tabbed-drawer pattern. The RAG **local-passage deep-link UX is built and proven**. The approval **risk grade is already on the wire at render time** (`riskTier` + `gateBehavior`). The whole redesign is therefore a *re-seat onto existing substrate + one genuinely new answer-event carrier*, not a new framework.

## §2 Thesis — the content analog of 561's surface unification

**561 unified the SURFACE** — one window, made true by construction (the `interaction-surface` gate forbids a second visible interaction surface). **The remaining defect is the CONTENT tier**: the one window still renders divergent content authorities (above) — the **548 two-authorities class at the content/evidence tier**, with the agent path as the impoverished fork of the RAG path.

**The correct structure: ONE authority per content concept, with the agent's forks subsumed, so that — in EVERY mode, by construction —**
1. an answer that claims grounding carries **verifiable, clickable, local-passage citations** (inline marks + a source-chip row + a sources pane + click-to-the-exact-local-line);
2. **status reads semantically** through one status→tone authority;
3. **the answer renders once** (one block, one reading measure) on **one ordered run timeline**.

561 made *two windows* unrepresentable; **565 makes *a grounded answer with no evidence projection*, and *a second grounded-answer authority*, unrepresentable.** Same kernel, same template, next tier down.

## §3 The correct structure (authority by authority — end-state grade)

### §3.A The one grounded-answer authority — the category-defining + differentiating piece

One canonical *"this answer was grounded by these sources"* record carried on the **answer event itself**, independent of whether the answer came from the RAG SPI or the agent loop. The correct structure generalises the RAG chain to both paths and collapses the three evidence renderers into one:

- **One answer↔source correlation.** Generalise `StreamingCitationMatcher` to run over the turn's collected `Hit`s in the agent loop (or have the LLM emit source markers reconciled against them). The agent stops *dropping* provenance.
- **One provenance carrier on the answer event.** `AgentDone` (and the RAG answer) carry the grounding set — the field RAG effectively has and the agent lacks. (This is the **new substrate** §7 names; everything else is reuse.)
- **One Evidence render authority.** Unify `CitationsPanel` + `searchEvidence` + `CitationHoverCard`'s ad-hoc scorer onto `evidenceProjection`, yielding one Evidence card + a **sources pane** in the one window's right-drawer (a fourth panel, or a tab beside the retrospective — the slot already supports it).
- **One deep-link path.** Wire the agent evidence to the existing `citation-select` → `highlightCitation`/`openExternal`.

**Result, by construction in any mode:** inline citations woven into the answer, a source-chip row beneath it, a sources pane, and click-to-the-exact-local-passage. And the inversion the category demands — *"show the evidence, hide the plumbing"*: the raw retrieval set stops being the primary content of a tool card and becomes the backing store the citation projection reads.

### §3.B The one run-status authority → semantic tone projection

Generalise the notices-only `severityToTone` into a lifecycle-**status**→tone authority; one status model consumed by **both** the inline card and the drawer (collapsing today's colour *and* model divergence); wire the plumbed-but-unused `AgentProgress.severity`; extend the existing colour-token gate so a status cannot render without its semantic tone token. PENDING/RUNNING/COMPLETED/REJECTED/FAILED read the same, everywhere.

### §3.C The one answer-presentation authority + one ordered run timeline

One answer block — reconcile markdown vs plain-text to **sanitised markdown + claim-marks** — with a **reading measure** (`ch`-based), for every mode. One **timestamp-ordered run timeline** rendering (progress + tool rows + reasoning + answer) from a *single* structure so ordering is correct by construction (fixes the two-structure defect), with **collapsed-expandable tool rows** (type-icon + verb+target + the §3.B status glyph) and a **collapsible reasoning disclosure** that streams then collapses. Honor `structuredData.mcpContent` (560).

### §3.D Approval as a risk→presentation projection (pure FE; risk already on the wire)

Low/medium risk → **inline, in-stream Approve/Deny** in the run timeline (keeps run context visible — the category default); high/irreversible → the existing modal + type-to-confirm **as the escalation**, not the default. The grade (`riskTier`/`gateBehavior`) is already present at render time, so this is a pure presentation decision — no backend change.

## §4 The differentiator — local passage-level citations, by subsuming the fork

NotebookLM and Perplexity cite *web pages*: they can only deep-link to a URL. **We own the corpus** — and the **local-passage deep-link already exists on the RAG path** (`citation-select` → `highlightCitation`/`openExternal`). Unifying the grounded-answer authority (§3.A) *extends that existing deep-link to every grounded answer*, so a citation opens the **exact local file at the exact line, highlighted** — the verification web tools structurally cannot do, and the affordance AnythingLLM's and Open WebUI's own communities are asking for and lack. We exceed the bar by **subsuming the fork**, not building anew.

## §5 What must NOT change
- The **IA** (one window, modes, posture, retrospective) — 561's gate-locked result.
- The underlying **records** (`Hit`/`ExcerptRegion`/`SearchTrace`/`ContextCitation`) — reuse, do not re-model; `evidenceProjection.ts` is the reuse spine.
- The **kernel + existing presentation gates** — extend (colour-token → status-tone; the evidence register), never fork a parallel framework.

## §6 Anti-drift — what (if anything) earns a new gate

Most of 565 rides **existing** gates: the colour-token closure extended to a status-tone authority (§3.B), layout-purity for the reading measure (§3.C), message-single-model for the toast/posture collision, the a11y/operability/adaptivity gates for the run timeline. The **one** candidate NEW gate is a **grounded-answer / evidence-surface gate** (sibling of `execution-surface` / `operation-surface` / `interaction-surface`): *a grounded answer rendered without an evidence projection, or a second grounded-answer authority, fails the build* — the content-tier analog of `interaction-surface`. Per the project's "only gate what earns it" + the structural-defects-don't-need-repeat-incidents rule (one documented "answer with no evidence projection" is enough to justify the structural fix), the **gate-vs-discipline choice is named explicitly as a closure decision, not defaulted.** Note **564** governs any new evidence *wire* surface (a `contract-surfaces.v1.json` row + regen; no hand-authored Zod); note **563** retired the `ux-audit-closure` gate → the measured audit is honor-system (§9).

## §7 De-risk / corrections log

**Correction of this file's first draft (same day).** The draft's load-bearing claim — *"the evidence layer is a projection of the existing `SearchTrace`"* — was wrong on two counts: (a) `SearchTrace` is ranking-*why*, not source content (the citable path/line/snippet ride on `Hit`/`ExcerptRegion`; the RAG citation record is `ContextCitation`); (b) the agent's `AgentDone.finalResponse` is a bare string that *drops* provenance before the answer. So §3.A is **partly new substrate** (the answer-event provenance carrier + a unified answer↔source matcher), which is in scope because it is the *structural* fix, not a patch.

**Confidence.** IA needs no restructuring: **HIGH**. Grounded-answer authority achievable on the existing spine: **MEDIUM** until the unknowns below are checked against code.

**Open unknowns to resolve before implementation.**
1. Can `StreamingCitationMatcher` be generalised over the agent's collected `Hit`s, or is LLM-emitted-marker reconciliation the better mechanism? (Determines the §3.A matcher shape.)
2. Does the markdown↔plain answer-block reconciliation (§3.C) disturb the existing claim-marks?
3. Does a second right-drawer (the sources pane) need mutual-exclusion arbitration? (None exists today; the slot merely stacks.)
4. The §6 gate-vs-discipline decision for the evidence-surface invariant.

## §8 Phasing (general — order, not slices; each independently shippable + bar-raising)

1. **Presentation pass** — status-tone unification (§3.B) + the single answer block + reading measure + the ordered run timeline (§3.C). Presentation-only, no backend, highest leverage / lowest risk.
2. **The grounded-answer authority** (§3.A) — the substrate piece: the answer-event provenance carrier + a unified answer↔source matcher + the unified Evidence render + the local-passage deep-link + the sources pane. The category-defining differentiator.
3. **Risk-escalated approval** (§3.D) — the FE projection of the on-wire grade.

## §9 Validation discipline (non-negotiable)

Every user-visible change is declared successful **only** when validated in the **real UI with the model loaded** — a real agent run driven live (as proven feasible 2026-06-03). Presentation work additionally takes the **measured** whole-screen UX audit (axe / contrast oracle, auditor ≠ committer) per the now-honor-system `ux-audit-closure` policy (gate retired in 563 — plan it explicitly). The evidence layer is specifically validated by **clicking a citation in a live answer and landing on the highlighted local passage** — the chain of evidence demonstrated, not asserted.

## §10 De-risk pass (2026-06-03) — code-level investigation that discharges §7 and corrects §3

A read-only, source-cited investigation of the exact seams §7 named, run before any implementation (mirrors 561 §8). It resolved every unknown and **corrected several §3 claims** — those corrections are authoritative over the body above.

**§3.A — the grounded-answer authority. CORRECTED: the RAG citation-matcher is NOT directly reusable on agent hits; the real work is a named chunk-identity decision, not "generalize the matcher."**
- `StreamingCitationMatcher`'s *authoritative* pass delegates to `DocumentService.matchCitations`, which (`RemoteDocumentService.matchCitations` → worker `CitationMatchOps.lookupChunkContent`) keys on **indexed-chunk identity (`parentDocId` + `chunkIndex`)** and looks the chunk's content/embedding up from the index. The agent's `KnowledgeSearchResponse.Hit` (and the `buildSearchEvidence` projection: `title`/`path`/`excerpt`/`line`) carries **no `parentDocId`/`chunkIndex`** — RAG chunks and search hits are different retrieval granularities. So you **cannot construct a usable `ContextCitation` from a `Hit`** for the authoritative pass; only the lexical draft (`matchSentenceLexical`, excerpt-only) would run. **The named decision (pick one, in scope):** (a) **thread chunk identity through the agent search path** (`SearchTool`/`buildSearchEvidence` carry `parentDocId`+`chunkIndex`) so a real `ContextCitation` is constructible and the existing authoritative matcher reuses *as-is* — the cleanest, makes the agent search carry the same identity RAG already has; (b) lexical-only attribution (weaker); (c) LLM-emitted source markers reconciled against the retained hits. **Likely silent failure if unguarded:** wiring empty `parentDocId`s → `lookupChunkContent` returns null → zero authoritative matches, green tests, dead feature.
- **Carrier — cheap, CONFIRMED.** The hits are already retained for the whole turn on `AgentSession.executedTools` (the full `OperationResult.structuredData` survives; only the LLM-context message is truncated) — needs a small package accessor. The carrier goes on `AgentEvent.AgentDone` + its **hand-shaped** SSE projection (`AgentController.toSsePayload`, a literal `Map.of(...)`); the FE hand-reads `data.finalResponse`. It is **NOT 564-governed** (no `contract-surfaces` row, no generated schema-type) → adding a `citations` field is low-cost, but it is *unguarded wire* (no generated parse-boundary validation — a deliberate choice to record).

**§4 — the differentiator. CONFIRMED, essentially free.** `citation-select` → `Shell.onCitationSelect` → `InspectorPane.highlightCitation` already opens an **arbitrary indexed path at a line** (`/api/preview?docId=<path>` → scroll to `startLine/endLine`); it does **not** require the doc to be pre-loaded. `host.platform.openExternal`/`revealInExplorer` also take arbitrary local paths (no OS-level line targeting). So unifying the grounded-answer authority extends a *working* local-passage deep-link to the agent — the differentiator carries essentially zero deep-link cost.

**§3.B — status authority. CORRECTED twice.** (1) It is **one status→tone *mapper*, not one status model**: the drawer History (`AgentSessionController.history[].success`, binary terminal, from the action-ledger) and the inline `ToolCall.status` (6-state live lifecycle, from SSE) are *legitimately* two models — but `ToolCall` already carries a redundant `success?` the History mirrors, so a shared `statusToTone(...)` (generalizing `SystemNotice.severityToTone`) consumed by both renders is the correct, cheap unification; a deeper model merge is not warranted. (2) **Enforcement needs a NEW gate, not an extension of `check-color-tokens`**: that gate bans bare colored *literals* only — History's inline `color: var(--accent-danger)` *passes* it, and theme-closure only checks the token is *defined*. Forcing "every status render routes through the mapper" requires a new ratchet gate (the `check-message-single-model` pattern), which is a real (small) cost, named here.

**§3.C — answer presentation. Split confidence.** (1) **Ordered run timeline → HIGH:** the canonical record is already one `occurredAt`-sorted `.map` (`unifiedThreadProjection`); the only "second structure" is the transient dedup-overlay, whose entries already carry `ConversationEntry.timestamp` (`Date.now()` at every append) — a merged ordered live timeline is a *localized* `UnifiedChatView`-render refactor, no missing data, no backend change (streaming tails pin to "now"). (2) **One answer block → MEDIUM (named fallback):** claim-marks are a RAG decoration built by `segmentText()` via `fullText.indexOf(sentenceText)` over **plain** text — markdown rendering destroys that (no flat string; syntax stripped; DOMPurify replaces nodes). Unifying on the markdown block forces claim-marks to be **re-implemented as a markdown-aware decoration** (a `marked` extension or post-parse DOM walk), ~75 lines, not a prop swap. **Named fallback:** make markdown-vs-plain an internal *render mode* of one unified block and gate claim-marks to the flat-text (RAG) path until the markdown-aware decoration lands — the "one block" structure holds even if grounded-span marking initially renders only in RAG mode. **Silent failure to guard:** a markdown answer carrying claims falls through `segmentText` to all-`ungrounded` with no error.

**§3.D — inline approval. Feasible, net-new UI.** The `INLINE_CONFIRM`/`TYPED_CONFIRM` grade is on the wire, but today **both render in the same modal** (`AuthorizationHost`); `INLINE_CONFIRM` means "one-click *inside* the modal," and the in-timeline approve affordance was deliberately removed (550 C3). An in-timeline low/medium approve is feasible **without** breaking the one-ceremony FIFO / fail-closed guarantees **iff** it resolves through the *same* broker `present()` promise and participates in the *same* queue/teardown — net-new UI, plumbing present.

**§7.3 — drawer arbitration.** No mutual-exclusion exists; the three right-drawer panels share one `flex-direction:column` slot, so two-open-at-once **already** overlaps (a pre-existing latent bug, logged to `observations.md`; `AdvisoryInboxDrawer` doesn't even `display:none` when closed). The sources pane needs a thin **single-drawer arbiter** (opening one closes the others) + the `display:none`-when-closed convention — low cost, and it fixes the latent bug.

**Live dev-server probes (the plan's empirical leg) — status.** Probe A (agent search evidence carries `path`+`line`) is **already confirmed** by code (`buildSearchEvidence`) and by the earlier live run (the tool card showed `filename · line N · excerpt`). Probe B (the RAG deep-link opens+highlights an arbitrary local file) is **code-confirmed** (§4 above) end-to-end; a live click remains a belt-and-suspenders check. **Probe C (a measured axe/contrast baseline of the live agent window) is OUTSTANDING** — it genuinely needs the running stack, which at de-risk time was owned by another session (OWNER_CONFLICT); it sizes the §3.B/§3.C token+contrast work and satisfies the §9 measured-audit baseline, but does not change the design. Deferred pending stack availability.

**Corrected confidence (post-de-risk).**

| Part | Pre | Post | The remaining decision / residual risk |
|---|---|---|---|
| §3.A grounded-answer authority | MEDIUM | **MEDIUM-HIGH** | the chunk-identity decision (thread-identity vs lexical vs LLM-marker) — named, not open; carrier + hits confirmed cheap |
| §3.B status→tone | MEDIUM-HIGH | **HIGH** | the enforcement gate is a separate (small) new-gate decision |
| §3.C ordered timeline | MEDIUM | **HIGH** | none material |
| §3.C one answer block | MEDIUM | **MEDIUM** | claim-marks markdown-aware reimpl (named fallback exists) |
| §3.D inline approval | MEDIUM-HIGH | **HIGH (net-new UI)** | must hook the broker promise/FIFO correctly |
| §4 differentiator | — | **HIGH (free)** | none — the deep-link already opens arbitrary path+line |

**Net:** no part is blocked; the one genuine substrate decision (§3.A chunk-identity) is now *named with three concrete options* rather than an open unknown, and the highest-value piece (the differentiator) is confirmed essentially free. The outstanding item is the measured contrast baseline (Probe C), which sizes work but does not gate the design.

## §11 Implementation outcome (2026-06-03)

Implemented on `worktree-565-agent-window` (commits `9bffd8c..`); live validation deferred to one final batch per the standing rule.

**Phase 1 (presentation pass).** `shell-v0/utils/statusTone.ts` — the ONE status→tone→accent authority (NoticeTone vocabulary single-sourced from `SystemNotice`), adopted by `ToolCallCard` (the status word) + `RetrospectivePanel` (History) + the previously-dangling `AgentProgress.severity` (progress rows). The agent run renders by authoritative `timestamp` (one ordered timeline). The canonical answer block is `jf-markdown-block` for every mode (the RAG flat-text+claims block kept only when claims are present), with a 74ch reading measure. `ToolCallCard` auto-collapses terminal cards.

**Phase 2 (the grounded-answer authority — the differentiator).** Chosen option (a): the agent search `Hit` carries chunk identity, so `SearchTool.buildSearchEvidence` was enriched with `parentDocId`/`chunkIndex`/`startLine`/`endLine`, `AgentSession.collectGroundingSources()` dedups the run's citable hits, and `AgentStepRunner.groundedDone()` attaches them to every `AgentDone`. `AgentCitationResolver` reuses the EXISTING authoritative `DocumentService.matchCitations` over the answer (4s timeout, degrades to source-only — never silent-zero), late-bound via `AgentLoopService.setCitationDocumentService` ← `AgentLoopWiring` ← `OrchestrationPhase`. `AgentDone` gained `sources` + `citations` (carried on the hand-shaped SSE, non-564). FE: `<jf-sources-pane>` (a right-drawer cloning the retrospective pattern) renders the answer's sources as clickable cards that dispatch the existing `citation-select` → `highlightCitation`, **opening the exact local file at the highlighted line** — the differentiator, working.

**Phase 3 (prevention).** `rightDrawerArbiter.ts` — the single-drawer arbiter the retrospective + sources panes register with (fixes the logged latent overlap bug; §7.3). Risk-graded approval (§3.D) implemented as a **risk-graded *presentation* of the ONE ceremony host**, NOT per-card buttons: low/medium (`gateBehavior != TYPED_CONFIRM`) render as a non-blocking bottom card (the run stays visible), high keeps the full modal — preserving 550 C3's single broker/FIFO/fail-closed authority (the structural synthesis: §3.D's intent + 550 C3's centralization, no regression).

**Resolved §6 gate-vs-discipline decision → DISCIPLINE, not a hard gate.** A precise status-tone gate is **not feasible**: lifecycle-status coloring is syntactically indistinguishable from the 30+ legitimate static semantic-colour CSS uses (`.err`, `.outcome-FAILED`, score colours), so a hard scan would false-positive massively (and the project avoids enumerated allowlists). The status-tone authority is enforced by the `statusTone.ts` module + its adoption + the unit test + this design rule — the same `prose-only` tier as most presentation rules. The candidate `evidence-surface` gate is likewise discipline (a grounded answer's source-attachment is a runtime property; `groundedDone()` is the single emission seam by construction). Recorded here per §6's "name the choice explicitly."

**Follow-up refinements — IMPLEMENTED + live-validated (2026-06-04).** The three named §157 deferrals are now complete (commit set continues `9bffd8c..`); each was driven live in the real browser with the local model (zero console errors throughout):
1. **The per-sentence inline `[n]` superscript RENDERING on the markdown answer (the §3.C named follow-up).** `MarkdownBlock` gained a `citations: MarkdownCitation[]` input + a post-parse DOM walk (`decorateCitations`) that locates each cited sentence by a whitespace-tolerant, marker-stripped match across the rendered (markdown) text nodes and splices a `.cite-ref` superscript at the sentence boundary — preserving markdown while weaving in grounding. `UnifiedChatView.agentAnswerCitations` resolves the agent's `AgentSentenceCite`+`AgentSource` into the marks; click reuses the `citation-select` deep-link, hover reuses `CitationHoverCard` (via the extended `onCiteRefHover`). A cited sentence that can't be located is skipped gracefully (still in the Sources pane). Live: two inline marks rendered on a real answer; click opened `discipline-gate-kernel.md` at the line (`/api/preview` 200); hover fired. Unit: 4 `MarkdownBlock.test.ts` cases (match / graceful-skip / cross-emphasis / click).
2. **Record-persistence of the agent answer's sources across reload.** `AgentRunStore.toPayload` now persists `sources`/`citations` on the `done` event; `AgentInteractionMapper.fromRunEvent` projects them into the `ASSISTANT_MESSAGE` attributes (mirroring the RAG path's `claimMatches` at `ConversationEngine.persistedAssistant`), so they ride the canonical `/api/thread/{id}` record. FE: the record-half (`renderUnifiedItem`) renders the markdown answer with inline marks FROM `it.attributes.sources/citations`, and `hydrateAnswerEvidenceFromRecord` rehydrates the controller so the Sources pane + the `Sources · N` affordance render on reload. Live: after reload, `answerSources`/`answerCitations` rehydrated from the record, 2 inline marks rendered, `Sources · 1` shown, and a post-reload citation click opened the file. Unit: `AgentInteractionMapperTest.doneCarriesGroundingEvidence`.
3. **Folding the advisory + agent-activity drawers into the single-drawer arbiter (§7.3).** `AgentActivityPanel` + `AdvisoryInboxDrawer` now `registerRightDrawer(...)` and `closeOtherRightDrawers(...)` on open; `AdvisoryInboxDrawer` also gained `:host(:not([open])){display:none}` (the logged latent overlap bug — it kept a full-height flex slot when closed). Live: opening any of sources / agent-activity / advisory auto-closes the others (bidirectional), and the advisory drawer is `display:none` when closed.

---

## §12 The COMPOSITION tier — the run renders as one ordered, answer-first, dense projection (design theory 2026-06-04 → SHIPPED 2026-06-04)

> **As-built pointer (2026-06-04).** §12 is now IMPLEMENTED + live-verified — see **§12.11** (per-phase outcome) and **§12.12** (residuals, deliberate divergences & lessons). The body below (§12.1–§12.7) is the original forward-looking design; where it differs from **§12.10** (de-risk corrections) or §12.11/§12.12, the later sections are authoritative (the dated-history discipline). Notably: the dedup of two structures **persists** (§12.3.A was corrected — the unification is at the render model); the prominence collapse uses native `<details>`, **not** `OverflowController` (§12.3.C corrected); the layout is the **three-zone composition**, not a centred reading column (§12.3.D corrected by Probe R); grounding is the **persistent rail** (the chip-row alternative in §12.3.E was not built); and §12.6 landed as **register + early-warning**, not a hard gate (§12.10).

The CONTENT tier above shipped, and a live visual read of the result exposed the *next* structural defect — one tier down. §0–§11 made the agent answer **correct and grounded** (it carries verifiable local-passage citations, semantic status, one ordered run). But **how that content is composed on screen** is wrong: the run renders through oversized, empty, contextless tool cards that **bury the very answer we made verifiable**. §12 is the correct long-term design for that — the **composition tier** — and it completes the lineage **559 (presentation *values*) → 561 (the *surface*) → §0–§11 (the *content*) → §12 (the *composition*)**. Same correct-design register: feasibility disregarded, major re-seats in scope, end-state grade. Every current-behaviour claim below is verified against source (a 3-front investigation, 2026-06-04).

### §12.0 Scope
**In:** how the one window's run is *composed visually* — the ordered timeline, the tool-call rendering, the answer's prominence, the evidence spine, the density/hierarchy of the whole run. **Out (reuse, never re-model):** the content authorities (§0–§11 — what the answer/status/sources **are**) and the surface (561 — the one window). This tier is strictly the **render composition** of that content.

### §12.1 Diagnosis — composition is the UNPROJECTED facet; the run renders through TWO authorities
The root defect is the one **559 itself already named**: the presentation engine projects element **membership + value facets** (label via `present()`, colour/density via `token()`, tri-state observed-state, landmark, overflow-priority) through typed seams — and *those facets have never drifted* (Tier-2 ceiling reached). But the **rendered composition** — DOM structure, hierarchy, density, reading order, relative prominence — is **hand-authored in Lit templates** (Tier-4, grep-only) and therefore **keeps drifting**. **No authority owns hierarchy / density / composition.** That gap manifests as the **548 two-authorities class at the RENDER tier:**
- A tool call renders through **two** authorities — the live `ToolCallCard` (compact, collapsible, evidence-bearing) and the record-half `UnifiedChatView.renderToolActivity` (a *static* `🔧 tool · status` label in a `.message.assistant` box — no tool name, no verb/target, no collapse). The record path produces the **oversized empty cards** (measured live: **181 px tall for an 18-char label**; another **411 px**), so the answer is **buried below ~600 px** of near-empty boxes.
- The run is assembled by **dedup of two overlaid structures** (live `conversation[]` + record `projectUnifiedThread(unifiedEvents)`), not one ordered projection — "one ordered run" is *reconciled*, not *constructed*; the divergent tool rendering is downstream of that fork.
- So §3.C's "compact collapsed tool rows (icon + verb+target + status glyph)" landed in `ToolCallCard` but **not on the surface that actually renders** — because composition has no authority to land in.

> **Correction (§13.0, 2026-06-05):** "559 itself already named" overstates. **559 §8 deliberately EXCLUDED layout composition** ("the engine owns the cross-cutting element classes where the authorities apply; it does NOT own layout composition") — it left composition to hand-authored templates *on purpose*, not as a named-but-deferred facet. So the gap is 559's deliberate boundary, not an unfinished 559 item. §12 then projected the run's *prominence facet* + the *one-ordered-run projection* (closing the render-tier two-authorities defect this section names), but the **spatial** composition (the zone frame, the run-as-visual-timeline spine, the margin balance) stayed hand-authored. **§13 is the principled refinement of 559 §8's boundary** that brings *projected-content* composition under an authority while leaving *bespoke-leaf* composition hand-authored.

### §12.2 Thesis — the composition tier completes the presentation engine
The correct structure is to **extend the presentation engine to PROJECT COMPOSITION**: the run is **one ordered projection** of a typed timeline, each item rendered at a **declared prominence/density** through **one tool-call presentation authority**, **composed answer-first** with **ambient grounding** — so the *buried-answer / oversized-empty-card / two-tool-render-path / sparse-layout* classes become **unrepresentable by construction**. Unifying principle: **answer-first, audit-on-demand; grounding ambient.** The answer + its citations lead; the run is a dense, collapsible audit trace; the evidence (our differentiator) is omnipresent, not modal. This is where every mature answer-engine / agentic surface converged — reached by *closing 559's gap*, NOT a parallel framework.

### §12.3 The correct structure (authority by authority)
- **§12.3.A One ordered run projection — collapse the live/record fork.** The run is a single ordered projection of the canonical interaction record (`InteractionEvent`/`occurredAt`); the live SSE is the in-flight **tail of the same projection**, not a second render path. One projection → one render → the dedup-of-two-structures (and its divergent tool rendering) disappears. Reuses `unifiedThreadProjection` + `InteractionEvent.occurredAt`; the 561 P-A "projection-not-fork" discipline.
- **§12.3.B One tool-call presentation authority — the compact row.** A single tool-call render primitive: a **dense row** — type-icon + **verb + target** + outcome + duration + the §3.B status glyph — **expandable** to detail (args/output/evidence). Both halves render through it; `renderToolActivity`'s static-label fork is retired. The verb+target is **projected via the Display authority** (`present()` over the operation ref — the existing 557 pattern), so the row reads *"searched ‘discipline-gate kernel' → 1 result"* / *"ingest …-kernel.md · denied"*, never *"tool · status"*. Kills the oversized-empty-card class; reuses `ToolCallCard`'s collapse.
- **§12.3.C The composition/prominence facet — the missing 559 facet.** Each timeline item **declares its prominence** (answer = primary; tool = secondary/dense; reasoning = tertiary/collapsible; progress = ambient), and the surface composes them **answer-first** — the answer leads, the run recedes (collapsible to a one-line summary — *"3 steps · 1 source · 1 denied"* — once the answer lands). Density/prominence become **declared facets of the presentation engine**, not hand-authored padding/min-height. Closes 559's named gap; reuses `OverflowController` / progressive-disclosure + the `--density-*` scale.
- **§12.3.D The reading column + three-zone composition.** The conversation **adopts the reading measure** (`SurfaceLayout` `data-fill="reading"` — *declared but currently UNADOPTED*; likely a narrower run-specific measure per 559 Appendix A's A/B finding) so content stops sprawling/left-aligning full-width. The window composes **three zones** — run-trace spine (left margin) · conversation column (centre) · evidence rail (right) — balancing the wide canvas instead of dead gutters.
- **§12.3.E Ambient grounding — the evidence spine.** The answer's evidence is a **persistent projection**: a source-chip row directly under the answer + a **persistent (default-shown) evidence rail**, **cross-highlighted** with the inline `[n]` marks — not a modal toggle that leaves an empty gutter. Reuses the §3.A grounded-answer authority + `evidenceProjection`.
- **§12.3.F The trace spine — one ordered run made visual.** The ordered timeline renders with a **status-coloured vertical spine** (the §3.B status-tone authority projected onto the trace), the answer as the terminal node — making "one ordered run" visible and status scannable at a glance.

### §12.4 The differentiator — the dense, verifiable audit trace
Answer engines *collapse* steps to hide them; we collapse them to **subordinate** them while keeping each step's evidence one expand away and deep-linked to the exact local passage. Answer-first **and** audit-on-demand **and** grounding-always-visible is the trust surface the field lacks.

### §12.5 What must NOT change
The content authorities (§0–§11) and the surface (561) — reuse, never re-model. The status-tone, evidence, and Display projections — **extend**, never fork. The presentation gates (557/558/559) — extend with the composition facet, never a parallel framework.

### §12.6 Anti-drift — the register + the gate-vs-discipline decision (named, not defaulted)
The **gate-able** invariants (the deepest causes): (a) **one tool-call renderer** — forbid a second tool-call render path outside the single authority (the live/record fork); (b) **one ordered run projection** — forbid a second run-assembly structure. These follow the proven kernel (declaration → governed projection → register-backed gate; 553 execution-surface, 561 interaction-surface) — an extended or new surface register + a gate making the fork unrepresentable. The **discipline** part (named per the §6 status-tone precedent, where a precise gate proved infeasible): prominence/density **tuning** is judgment — held by the *declared composition primitive + adoption + the existing `check-layout-purity` / `check-adaptive-closure` gates + the measured UX-audit discipline*. Record the gate-vs-discipline choice as a closure decision, not a default.

### §12.7 Phasing (general — order, not slices; each independently shippable + bar-raising)
1. Collapse the tool-render fork → **one compact tool-call row authority** (highest-leverage visible win; eliminates the empty cards).
2. **One ordered run projection** (retire the dedup-of-two-structures).
3. The **composition/prominence facet + answer-first hierarchy + the trace spine**.
4. The **reading column + three-zone layout + the ambient grounding rail**.
5. The **register + gate** (anti-drift) + the gate-vs-discipline record.

### §12.8 Reuse spine (confirmed by the 2026-06-04 investigation — do NOT reinvent)
`primitives/surfaceLayout.ts` (`data-fill="reading"`, declared-unadopted; gate `check-layout-purity.mjs`) · `primitives/adaptiveBar.ts` `OverflowController` + `governance/adaptive-regions.v1.json` + `check-adaptive-closure.mjs` (collapse-to-fit / progressive disclosure) · `components/chat/ToolCallCard.ts` (the compact render to make the single authority; `renderToolActivity` is the fork to retire) · `views/unifiedThreadProjection.ts` + `InteractionEvent.occurredAt` (the one ordered projection) · §3.A's `statusTone.ts` / `evidenceProjection.ts` / `SourcesPane.ts` (status + evidence projections) · `present()` (557 Display authority — the verb+target projection) · register/gate precedents `governance/{execution,operation,interaction}-surfaces.v1.json` + their `check-*.mjs`.

### §12.9 Validation discipline
Every user-visible change validated **live** (real browser + local model) and **measured** (axe / contrast + a measured read that the window leads with the answer, the trace is dense, grounding is ambient) — per §9 and the now-honor-system UX-audit discipline (563 retired the gate).

### §12.10 De-risk pass (2026-06-04) — discharges §12's unknowns against source + a live measurement, and CORRECTS §12.3
A read-only, source-cited investigation (3 fronts) plus one live measurement (Probe R), run before any implementation — the §12 analog of §10. It resolved every uncertainty and **corrected several §12.3 claims; those corrections are authoritative over the §12 body above.**

- **§12.3.A — CORRECTED (still tractable).** The `/api/thread` record refreshes **terminal-only** (`refreshUnifiedThread` fires on `ctrl.send(...).then(...)`, not per-event), so the live overlay is *necessary* mid-run and the **dedup PERSISTS** — the unification is **at the render MODEL** (extract a `projectLiveAgentActivity()` mirroring `unifiedThreadProjection.projectUnifiedThread`, so both halves emit `UnifiedTurnItem` and render through **one** item renderer). What dies is the divergent *tool* rendering, not the two sources. The live `conversation[]` is ~70 % shape-aligned with `ThreadEvent` (kinds map 1:1; gaps = ms↔ISO timestamp, local↔backend id, flat↔`attributes`), and a shadow projection already exists in `renderLiveAgentActivity` (the dedup+sort). **Not** a streaming-projector rebuild. (Refutes the §12.3.A phrasing "eliminating the dedup".)
- **§12.3.B — CORRECTED (small net-new, not pure reuse).** Two real gaps: (1) `present()` returns a **label only** — it does *not* compose "verb + target" (`display/present.ts`); composing *"searched X" / "ingest Y"* from the operation id + arguments is net-new (a small `composeToolLabel()`). (2) `AgentInteractionMapper.fromRunEvent` **drops `arguments`** from the `TOOL_ACTIVITY` attributes (they ARE in the persisted `tool_call_pending` payload, `AgentRunStore.java:584`, but not mapped) — so a reloaded thread cannot show the target without a one-line mapper fix (mirrors the §B sources fix). `structuredData` (evidence) **does** survive to reload. The compact row needs a normalized `ToolCallRow` shape both the live `ToolCall` and the record attributes produce.
- **§12.3.C — REFUTED (an error in §12.3.C).** `OverflowController` (`primitives/adaptiveBar.ts`) is a **horizontal bar-overflow** primitive (measures `offsetWidth`, overflows lowest-priority items to "…"); it is **NOT** a vertical run-collapse. The correct reusable mechanism is the **toggle-disclosure** already in `ToolCallCard` (`expanded`) / `RetrospectivePanel` (`open`) / native `<details>`. "Declared prominence" is a small typed `prominence` field on the timeline-item kind read by the renderer (net-new but typed).
- **§12.3.D — CORRECTED by Probe R (measured live, 2026-06-04).** At a real **2400 px** viewport: the conversation column (`.answer-plane`) is **full-bleed 2316 px**; the answer block already carries a **good measure — 558 px ≈ 80 ch** (14 px font); but assistant wrappers/tool cards span `max-width:95 %` (~2200 px). So the answer occupies **~24 % of the column** (≈76 % empty to its right) while the cards sprawl — the defect is **imbalance + a full-bleed column**, NOT the answer measure (which is fine — do not constrain it further). A/B: forcing a **760 px centered** column balanced answer↔cards but left **~68 % empty margins on both sides** — confirming 559 App.A's empty-margin tradeoff is real and *worse* at narrower measures. **Conclusion:** a centered reading column alone *wastes* the margins; the correct §12.3.D structure is the **three-zone layout (trace-spine | conversation | evidence-rail) that consumes the margins productively** — net-new layout, NOT `SurfaceLayout` (single-column only) and NOT a bare reading-measure adoption. (`SurfaceLayout`'s `data-fill="reading"` 72 rem is the wrong measure here; the answer measure already exists.)
- **§12.3.E — CONFIRMED tension.** A persistent always-shown sources rail conflicts with the single-drawer arbiter (`state/rightDrawerArbiter.ts` — opening one drawer closes the others), so it must live **outside** the arbiter'd `OverlayHost` drawer slot (a new structural housing) **or** "ambient grounding" reframes to the always-visible **source-chip row under the answer** + the pane stays a toggle. No `selectedSourceId` cross-highlight state exists today (net-new, small).
- **§12.6 — CORRECTED to register + DISCIPLINE (not a hard gate).** A second tool-renderer that re-models tool data *without importing the canonical type* is **import-invisible** — the same grep ceiling as `check-controls-a11y`. A `run-renderers` register enforces **adoption / early-warning** (and review on a declared second renderer), not absolute prevention. Same honest limit as the §3.B status-tone gate; name register+discipline, not a hard gate.

**Corrected confidence (post-de-risk):**

| Part | Pre | Post | Residual |
|---|---|---|---|
| §12.3.A one ordered run projection | MEDIUM | **HIGH** | a model-level `projectLiveAgentActivity()`; dedup persists by design |
| §12.3.B one compact tool-call row | MEDIUM | **MEDIUM-HIGH** | small net-new: carry `arguments` in the mapper + a `composeToolLabel()` + the normalized `ToolCallRow` |
| §12.3.C prominence + collapse | LOW-MEDIUM | **MEDIUM-HIGH** | toggle-disclosure (not OverflowController); a typed `prominence` field |
| §12.3.D layout | LOW-MEDIUM | **MEDIUM** | three-zone is net-new layout; answer measure already correct; the margins are the trace+rail (not centering) |
| §12.3.E ambient grounding | MEDIUM | **MEDIUM-HIGH** | rail outside the arbiter OR chip-row reframe; + `selectedSourceId` |
| §12.6 anti-drift | MEDIUM | **HIGH** | register + discipline (gate is early-warning, not absolute) |

**Net:** no part is blocked. The one structural correction worth surfacing — Probe R's measured result — is that the **answer measure is already right; the layout fix is the three-zone composition that fills the wide-viewport margins with the trace spine + evidence rail, not a centered reading column.** The §12.3.A unification is a model-level refactor (the dedup stays), §12.3.B/C/E are small net-new pieces over reuse, and §12.6 is register-backed discipline. Implementation can proceed against §12.7's phasing with these corrections folded in.

## §12.11 Implementation outcome (2026-06-04)

Implemented on `worktree-565-agent-window` (commits `d5539ad..`), one phase per commit, each user-visible phase live-validated in the real browser with the local model on the lease-free stack (zero console errors throughout). **No merge to `main`** (per the standing constraint). The §12.10 corrections were folded in as written.

**Phase 1 — one compact tool-call row authority (§12.3.B).** `AgentInteractionMapper.fromRunEvent` now emits a `tool_call_proposed` `TOOL_ACTIVITY` carrying `callId/toolName/arguments/risk` for every tool (completed/rejected events carry no identity — proposed does) and carries `arguments` on `tool_call_pending`; `unifiedThreadProjection` collapses tool activity by **MERGE-per-callId** (was keep-latest) so identity + outcome land on one row. New `display/toolLabeling.ts` `composeToolLabel()` humanizes the wire name + extracts the salient target. `UnifiedChatView.renderToolActivity` builds a normalized `ToolCall` from the record attributes and renders the SAME `<jf-tool-call-card>` the live half uses — retiring the static `🔧 tool · status` fork. The white-space:pre-wrap shadow-inheritance bloat (measured 442/426px empty cards) was the root cause of the oversized cards; reset on `.message.assistant`. Live: live + reloaded record both render compact ~70px rows; arguments survive into the record.

**Phase 2 — one ordered run projection (§12.3.A).** New `projectLiveAgentActivity()` mirrors `projectUnifiedThread` (both emit `UnifiedTurnItem`); a `tool-call-group` EXPANDS to one tool-activity item per callId. `renderUnifiedConversation()` is the single merge point (record + live, deduped — record wins, terminal-only per §12.10), rendered through the ONE `renderUnifiedItem`; `renderLiveAgentActivity`/`renderAgentEntry`/`renderAgentToolCard` retired. Live: a live run and the reloaded record render the IDENTICAL ordered timeline `[user, progress, progress, tool, progress, tool, progress, assistant]` — no double-render.

**Phase 3 — prominence facet + status-coloured trace spine + run-collapse (§12.3.C/F).** A typed `prominence` facet on `UnifiedTurnItem` (primary/secondary/ambient), declared by both projections. `renderTimeline` composes answer-first: primary items render at full prominence as direct conversation children; each run of secondary/ambient items collapses into ONE status-coloured trace spine (node tinted by the §3.B `statusAccent`), via native `<details>` disclosure (the §12.10 correction — NOT `OverflowController`), auto-collapsing to a one-line summary ("2 steps · 1 denied") once the answer lands. Live: the trace auto-collapsed on answer; the pure `/api/thread` record rendered the same collapsed, answer-first composition.

**Phase 4 — three-zone layout + persistent ambient grounding rail (§12.3.D/E).** A new `state/selectedSource.ts` shared store keys the cross-surface selection by the source's local-passage identity. `SourcesPane` gained a `docked` mode (the §12.10 correction — the persistent rail is the SAME component as the toggle drawer, NOT a fork; mounted OUTSIDE the single-drawer arbiter so it never closes when other drawers open). `MarkdownBlock`'s inline `[n]` marks carry `data-cite-key` and highlight in sync with the rail card. `UnifiedChatView`: at ≥64rem the conversation column hugs the reading measure + the rail consumes the right margin, the group centred (Probe R: the answer measure was already right; the fix fills margins, not a centered column). Live (1980px): grounded run renders the answer + persistent "Sources · 2" rail (79px gap, balanced ~500px margins, no overflow); bidirectional cross-highlight (inline `[n]` ↔ rail card) + the rail-card deep-link opens the local passage while the rail PERSISTS. **Honest scope:** the separate "source-chip row under the answer" (§12.10 framed as "rail OR chip-row") was not built — the rail is the stronger structural choice and the inline marks are the under-answer references; the §12.3.D trace-spine-in-the-left-margin is approximated by Phase 3's collapsed inline trace + the balanced left margin.

**Phase 5 — the run-renderers register + the §12.6 gate-vs-discipline decision → register + EARLY-WARNING (not a hard gate).** `governance/run-renderers.v1.json` declares the canonical authorities (one tool-call primitive `jf-tool-call-card` + its `composeToolLabel` label authority; one run projection `projectUnifiedThread`/`projectLiveAgentActivity`) and their allowed consumer sites. `scripts/ci/check-run-renderers.mjs` (cloning the `check-message-single-model` scripts/ci pattern) flags a second mount of the tag / a second importer of the label or projection outside the register — wired into `ci.yml` + the CLAUDE.md pre-merge list. **Proven, not a no-op:** a fork probe (a file mounting `<jf-tool-call-card>` + importing the projection) trips the gate on both counts; removing it passes. **The §12.10 honest limit holds:** a re-model that hand-rolls its own tool-card markup or run assembly WITHOUT importing the canonical symbols is import-invisible and slips the grep — so this is register + discipline, paired with the §12.9 measured UX-audit. **No tier-register row** was added: the precedent (the sibling 559 scripts/ci presentation gates carry no tier-register rows — only prose *disciplines* like row #31 do) and the "Before Appending to CLAUDE.md" broad-applicability test (the rule is slice-specific) both say the decision belongs here + in the register + the script header, not in `.claude/rules/tier-register.md`.

**Final verification (whole worktree, 2026-06-04).** FE `tsc` clean · FE unit `2398 passed` (242 files; +24 across the five phases: `toolLabeling`, `projectLiveAgentActivity` + prominence, `selectedSource` store, `SourcesPane` docked/cross-highlight, `MarkdownBlock`) · backend `:modules:app-agent:test` BUILD SUCCESSFUL (the Phase-1 mapper) · presentation gates green (`layout-purity`, `a11y-closure`, `controls-a11y`, `adaptive-closure`, `color-tokens`, `theme-token-closure`, `presentation-purity`, `strip-token-fallbacks`) · `run-renderers` green (+ fork-probe trip) · `prose-tier-register` + `check-workflow-triggers` green. Clean tree; five commits `d5539ad..e56be7c`.

## §12.12 Residuals, deliberate divergences & lessons (post-implementation, 2026-06-04)

The five phases landed every §12.7 item; this records what the **build** revealed that the **design** did not — the honest close-out, so a later reader trusts §12.11's "done" without re-deriving the deltas. This is the §12 analog of §B (the CONTENT tier's follow-up record).

**The root cause was more precise than §12.1 diagnosed — and the precise version is the reusable lesson.** §12.1 attributed the oversized empty cards (it cited 181/411 px) to the static-label record fork sitting in a `.message.assistant` box. Live measurement in Phase 1 found the *mechanism*: `.message { white-space: pre-wrap }` — correct for raw user text — **inherits across the shadow boundary** into `<jf-tool-call-card>`, so the card template's source-newlines render as ~200 px of visible vertical whitespace (the cards measured 442/426 px). Retiring the fork was necessary but **not sufficient**; the collapse also required `white-space: normal` on the assistant wrapper. The generalizable lesson (wider than this slice): **`white-space` is an inherited property that crosses shadow-DOM boundaries** — a host that slots whitespace-managing components must reset it, or the child's template newlines bloat the layout. Worth remembering for any future Lit host that wraps a component in a `pre-wrap` context.

**Deliberate divergences from §12.3 — decisions, not omissions:**
- **The source-chip-row under the answer (§12.3.E) — CLOSED, not deferred.** §12.10 framed grounding as "rail OR chip-row." The persistent rail is the stronger structural choice, and the inline `[n]` marks already sit *under the answer* as its references — a separate chip row would duplicate both surfaces. Not a follow-up; intentionally not built.
- **The trace-spine in the LEFT margin (§12.3.D/F) — DEFERRED as an optional refinement, with rationale.** The shipped three-zone is conversation-centre + rail-right, with the run trace rendered **inline + collapsed** (Phase 3), not a dedicated left-margin spine. Two reasons: (a) the trace is chronologically *between* the user turn and the answer — a fixed left-margin spine breaks that reading order, especially for multi-turn runs (multiple interleaved traces can't align to one margin); (b) Phase 3's collapse already delivers the recession §12.3.D wanted (the run is one summary line above a leading answer). The cost is honest: at *very* wide viewports (≳2200 px) the left margin is balanced whitespace, not trace-filled, so §12.3.D's "fill **both** margins" is only half-met (the right, by the rail). At typical 1280–1920 px the centred group reads balanced (validated: ~500 px margins each side at 1980 px). Moving the collapsed trace to the left margin is a marginal extreme-width gain against a real reading-order cost — left as an optional future refinement, not a defect.

**Error prominence is uniform (`secondary`) — defensible by the collapse trigger, not an oversight.** Every `error` item maps to `secondary`, so a tool error recedes into the collapsible trace. A *fatal* run error is **not** buried, though: the trace auto-collapses only **once the answer lands**, and a fatal error yields no answer → the trace stays open → the error is visible. Recoverable errors (the run continued to an answer) are correctly subordinated. So a separate fatal-error prominence tier was unnecessary — the collapse trigger already encodes the distinction.

**Validation limits (honest, so the "live-verified" claim is scoped):**
- The **narrow-viewport fallback** (< 64 rem: the rail hides, the "Sources · N" chip + toggle drawer return) was **not exercised live** — `resize_window` could not shrink the test viewport below the breakpoint (it stayed ~1980 px). It is deterministic CSS (base styles hide the rail / show the chip; the wide behaviour inverts only inside `@media (min-width: 64rem)`), and the wide path is thoroughly validated — but a live narrow-viewport pass is still owed.
- The **cross-highlight has a one render-tick lag on the rail side**: `MarkdownBlock` toggles its marks synchronously on the shared-store callback, but `SourcesPane` re-renders via Lit's async `requestUpdate`, so the matching rail card highlights on the next microtask (the unit test awaits `updateComplete` for this reason). Imperceptible in use; recorded so a future test/animation accounts for it.

**Closure discipline still owed (the one real open item).** Per the slice-execution rule — honor-system since 563 retired the `ux-audit-closure` gate — presentation-authority closure expects an **independent, *measured* (axe / contrast oracle, not eyeballed), live-verified whole-screen UX audit by an auditor ≠ committer**. This implementation was self-validated (committer = validator), which the rule explicitly says rests on the same blind spots as the implementation. **That independent measured audit is the remaining step before the branch is merge-ready; it is NOT done.** It is the right next action if/when this work is taken toward `main`.

## §12.13 Multi-turn defect pass (2026-06-04, commit `4368eaab`)

§12.12 admitted that every §12 live validation was **single-turn**. A critical-analysis re-read of the shipped code (turning that admission into action) found the worst defects hiding exactly there — in the **multi-turn** path (2+ user→answer cycles in one session) — and fixed them. This closes the "single-turn validation gap" as an *open* item.

- **(A) Per-segment trace collapse [HIGH, fixed + LIVE-PROVEN].** `renderRunTrace` keyed the collapse on ONE view-level toggle + the global `runActive` (`ctrl.isStreaming`) for every `<details>`, so a 2-turn session shared collapse state across runs (toggling one toggled all; an answered turn's trace re-opened while a later turn streamed). Fix: a `runTraceToggles` `Map<segId,bool>` + **derive the default from timeline structure** — a segment is open iff it is *trailing* (no `primary` item follows it = the in-flight run). `runActive` is gone. **Live-proven** on a self-assembled lease-free stack: two trace segments rendered with structurally-different defaults `[collapsed, open]`, and clicking one toggled ONLY it (`[false,true]` → click t1 → `[true,true]` → click t2 → `[true,false]`) — the exact bug, fixed.
- **(B) Per-answer live grounding [MEDIUM, fixed + unit-tested].** `projectLiveAgentActivity` attached the latest run's grounding (`ctrl.answerSources`) to EVERY `assistant-text`, so an earlier answer showed the current answer's `[n]` marks until reconcile. Fix: attach it to the LAST `assistant-text` only. Covered by a green regression test (`projectLiveAgentActivity` last-answer-only grounding). **Live grounding NOT exercised** — the self-assembled lease-free stack's inference connection was unstable ("AI Offline / Reconnecting"; the loaded model was Qwen3.5-9B and the agent's tool-calling LLM call returned `LLM_TRANSIENT` every run while a plain completion succeeded), so no run produced a grounded answer to click. That is an environment/model-config issue orthogonal to the FE projection; the behaviour is a pure-function projection the unit test pins.
- **(E) Trace summary [LOW, fixed + LIVE-PROVEN].** A tool-less run read "0 steps"; now the step count shows only when `tools>0`, else "N events" / "N error(s)" — observed live ("1 error" / "2 errors").
- **(C) `tool_call_proposed` [CLEARED, no change].** Suspected dead code; verified emitted (`AgentStepRunner:544`) + persisted + mapped (`AgentInteractionMapper:74`) + tested. A subagent audit misread the mapper switch AND the test file — recorded as a `critical-analysis-pass` reminder: read the code, don't trust the audit.
- Deferred (logged to `observations.md`): (D) message dedup by `kind+content`; (F) two `SourcesPane` instances at wide viewport.

**Validation status:** FE `tsc` + 2400 unit (incl. the 2 new multi-turn regression tests) + presentation gates green; **fix A and E live-proven** in the real browser; **fix B unit-proven, its live grounding blocked by an unstable self-assembled inference** (the shared dev stack was held by another agent, so a parallel lease-free stack was stood up for this pass — head+worker+inference on a separate port; the inference link proved flaky). A clean live grounding check on a stable stack is the small remaining follow-up. Lease-free launch lesson: a WMI-detached process gets a **stripped environment** (no `SystemRoot`/`TEMP`) and the JVM dies silently; launch via `Start-Process` (full env inherited) instead, and set `JAVA_HOME` to the **resolved** JDK path, not the scoop `current` junction (the agent-lessons junction trap).

## §12.14 Confidence / de-risk pass (2026-06-04)

A read-only confidence audit ranked the residual surprise-risks; a follow-up de-risk pass (investigate + experiment) closed some and **precisely isolated** the one real blocker. Net: confidence in the FE work went **up** — the thing that keeps failing is provably *not* the FE composition tier.

- **Merge-readiness — DE-RISKED (good).** `git merge-tree main HEAD` against current main (which has moved **44 commits**, mostly tempdoc-560) reports only THREE both-sides files: `ci.yml` and `CLAUDE.md` **auto-merge cleanly** (append-style additions at different anchors), and `docs/observations.md` has **one trivial append-collision** (both sides appended to the Inbox — resolve by keeping both). **No Java/FE conflicts** — the branch's `app-agent` + `ui-web` changes don't overlap main's changed set. Merge is low-risk.

- **Agent-LLM failure — ROOT CAUSE REFINED, blocker isolated to the head/environment (NOT the FE).** The §12.13 "unstable inference" was investigated. Findings: (1) the head's *canonical default* model is **Qwen3.5-9B** (`InferenceConfig.java:211`); my headless launcher loaded it because the override didn't take. (2) **Qwen tool-calling is NOT the problem** — a *direct* `tool_choice=required` request to llama-server returned a valid `search` tool-call. (3) Yet every *agent* run still failed `LLM_TRANSIENT` fast (~10 s, not a timeout) — so the failure is in the **head's STREAMING agent-LLM path** (`OnlineModeOps.streamChatWithTools`, with `tools` + `tool_choice=required` + `enable_thinking` `chat_template_kwargs`), **specific to Qwen** (whose 3.5 *thinking* tokens likely break the head's streaming tool-call parse); **Meta-Llama-3.1-8B — which the original 5-phase validation ran on — has no thinking mode and worked**. (4) **The model could not be pinned to Llama in the headless launch:** neither `JUSTSEARCH_VLM_MODEL` (env; not wired into `ResolvedConfigBuilder`) nor `-Djustsearch.llm.model_path=…Llama` (arrived in the JVM cmdline, *is* wired at `ResolvedConfigBuilder:897`, and the resolver *does* read sysprops at line 223) overrode the canonical default — a headless-vs-Tauri model-resolution gap worth a separate backend look. Per the plan's anti-thrash rule, the agent pursuit was stopped here. **Consequence:** fix-B's live grounding + the viewport rail checks (which need a completed grounded run) remain **blocked by the environment, not by the FE code** — and that isolation is itself the confidence gain.

- **Still owed (small, environment-gated):** the fix-B per-answer-grounding live check and the narrow-/wide-viewport rail checks should be run on a **stable agent stack** — the path of least resistance is the **dev-runner with Llama** (proper model wiring + the index already built) when the shared stack is free, not another hand-assembled headless head. The independent measured UX audit (§12.12) is still the merge-gating item.

**Confidence outcome:** HIGH on fix A/E (live-proven) and merge-readiness (measured); MEDIUM-HIGH on fix B (unit-proven + the live blocker proven external); the composition tier's end-to-end render was already live-proven single-turn in §12.11. The remaining live checks are gated on a working agent model, not on any open question about the FE work.

## §12.15 Remaining-work completion — §12.3.D/E built, §12.3.E ↔ chips, deferred bugs, measured UX audit (2026-06-04)

The user elected **full scope**: build the two deferred/closed design items (§12.3.D left-margin trace zone, §12.3.E source-chip-row) plus the deferred bugs, and validate live. The agent stack's *streaming* path was environment-blocked again (Llama loaded fine via `POST /api/settings/v2 {modelPath}` + `/api/inference/reload`, raw streaming tool-calls worked, yet the agent loop's LLM call still failed `LLM_TRANSIENT` — a head-side issue, not the model and not the FE). So, by the user's "implement now, validate later" choice, the FE was built + unit-tested and **live-validated by injecting a mock two-turn grounded conversation into the real UI** — which exercises the real components, CSS, and cross-highlight wiring (the rendering is independent of the LLM); only the real-LLM→data path is deferred.

- **§12.3.E source-chip-row — SHIPPED + live-proven.** A compact chip per grounding source (`[n] · filename`) under each grounded answer (a native `<button>`, controls-a11y-clean), the third ambient-grounding surface. All three surfaces (inline `[n]` · chips · rail) cross-highlight through the ONE `selectedSource` store; a chip click reuses the existing `citation-select` deep-link. **Live:** each answer rendered its OWN chip (turn-1 "Discipline-Gate Kernel", turn-2 "System Overview" — also confirming **fix B per-answer grounding** end-to-end); clicking turn-2's chip highlighted its chip + its rail card + its inline `[1]` mark, and NOT turn-1's (tri-surface sync, `[[false],[true]]` / rail `[true]` / inline `[true]`).
- **§12.3.D left run-spine — SHIPPED + live-proven (layout).** "One ordered run made visual": the latest run's steps as a persistent vertical status minimap (`statusAccent` nodes, the answer the terminal node) just-left of the centred conversation, wide-only, `aria-hidden` (decorative projection of the SAME `mergedTimeline()` so it can't diverge). **Live:** 2 status nodes + a terminal answer node, 8px from the conversation (adjacent, not lost in the margin), no horizontal overflow. **Honest residual (logged):** at very wide viewports (≳2000 px) the conversation+rail group is left-of-centre (left ~370 px vs right ~700 px) — the right margin is under-filled; the centring wants tuning. The §12.12 "fill BOTH margins" is now half-built (a left spine exists) but the wide balance is imperfect.
- **(D) occurrence-aware dedup + (F) one SourcesPane per viewport — SHIPPED.** (D) the live↔record message dedup is occurrence-aware so two identical consecutive turns no longer collapse (unit-tested). (F) the docked rail mounts only at the wide breakpoint (`matchMedia`); **live:** at the wide viewport the rail + spine render and the "Sources · N" chip is hidden; simulating narrow hid the rail + spine and brought back the "Sources · 1" chip — one SourcesPane per viewport.
- **§12.9 measured UX audit — RUN (axe-core, live).** Injected `axe-core@4.10` into the live agent UI (grounded answers + chips + rail + spine present) and ran WCAG 2.1 A/AA: **25 passes, 1 violation — and it is PRE-EXISTING, not the new work**: a `color-contrast` serious fail on the active affordance/autonomy-dial button (white `#ffffff` on accent-tint teal `#00d1b2` = 1.97:1, needs 4.5:1). The new chips/spine/rail are axe-clean. The pre-existing accent-contrast issue is logged to `observations.md` (out of 565-FE scope — an accent-token concern). **Caveat unchanged:** I am the committer, so this is a *measured self*-audit; an independent (auditor ≠ committer) measured pass remains the formal merge gate.

**Status:** every remaining FE item is implemented (commit on `worktree-565-agent-window`), unit-tested (2403 green), gate-clean, and live-validated for *rendering* via mock injection. Owed: a real-LLM end-to-end grounded run on a stable agent stack (the head-side agent-streaming blocker is environmental, separate from this FE work); the §12.3.D wide-margin tuning; the accent-contrast fix; and the independent UX audit.

## §12.16 Agent-stream blocker — diagnosis corrected, speculative backend fix REJECTED (2026-06-04)

A follow-up investigation into the `LLM_TRANSIENT` blocker (§12.15) produced a recommendation to *harden* the head's SSE consumer: `OnlineModeOps` raises `StreamTruncatedException` whenever `data: [DONE]` is absent, even when `finish_reason` is already a terminal value (`stop`/`tool_calls`/`length`); the agent loop is the only consumer with `requireSentinel=true`, so it alone fails against a backend that streams a complete tool turn without the sentinel. A change to treat *terminal-finish-reason-without-`[DONE]`* as success was drafted (a `isTerminalFinishReason` helper gating both the plain-stream and tool-stream `else if (requireSentinel)` branches).

**This change was implemented and then REVERTED. Do not re-attempt it as part of 565.** Reasons (decisive, in order):

1. **The premise is disproved by the investigation's own evidence.** The same investigation reported the agent run *completes fine on the dev-runner*. If llama-server universally omitted `[DONE]`, the dev-runner run would fail identically — it doesn't. So `[DONE]` is **not** being violated in practice; the blocker on the lease-free stack was **environmental** (the loaded model — the canonical-default Qwen's inline `<think>` tokens break the streaming tool-call parse; Meta-Llama-3.1-8B, no thinking mode, works). The proper unblock is **model-pinning at runtime, no code change** (`POST /api/settings/v2 {modelPath}` + `/api/inference/reload`).
2. **It breaks a deliberately documented contract.** `OnlineModeOps.streamChat(..., requireSentinel)`'s javadoc states `requireSentinel=true` ⇒ a missing `[DONE]` *must* raise `StreamTruncatedException`; the test `streamChat_capturesFinishReasonInTruncationException` enforces exactly the `finish_reason="length"` + no-`[DONE]` ⇒ truncation case the change would invert. Shipping it forces weakening that test — a hard-rule violation (`fix-root-causes-not-symptoms`).
3. **It is out of scope** for 565 (an FE presentation/evidence tempdoc) and rested on an **unreproduced** hypothesis (`audit-without-test` — a static throw-chain trace, not a repro against a known-good model).

If a *genuine* `[DONE]`-omission is ever observed with a known-good (non-thinking) model on a stable stack, that is a separate backend concern: it needs its own repro, its own decision about the documented `requireSentinel` contract, and its own regression test — not a ride-along in the 565 FE worktree.

**Per the GPU/stack coordination (another agent owned the live stack), the real-LLM grounded validation is explicitly DEFERRED by the user.** The mock-injection rendering validation (§12.15) + 2403 green unit tests stand; the real-LLM grounded run + §12.3.D wide-margin tuning + accent-contrast fix + independent measured UX audit remain the explicit pre-merge items. No merge to `main`.

## §12.17 Goal-driven gap closure — discipline→gate, the three-zone grid, and the live batch (2026-06-04)

A critical re-read of §12 against its own goals (the 561 analogy) found the *substance* achieved but two residuals between the stated ambition and the as-built — "unrepresentable by construction" was weaker than the title (the three unifications rested on discipline), and §12.3.D's "fill both margins" was half-met (the left run-spine was an absolute overlay, not a real zone). A `/goal`-driven pass (effort-irrelevant, structural-option-always, live-verification-last) closes them. Commits continue on `worktree-565-agent-window`; **no merge to `main`**.

**Phase A — the grounded-answer authority is now GATE-enforced (discipline→gate), `archunit`.** `AgentGroundingSeamAuditTest` (commit `c70854b2b`) asserts the grounding-carrying `AgentEvent.AgentDone` constructors (the 6-arg/7-arg overloads taking the `sources`/`citations` lists) are invoked ONLY from `AgentStepRunner.groundedDone()` — exempting the record's own ctor delegations and `AgentEventTracing`'s trace pass-through (which *copies* existing grounding, never *attaches*). A second site emitting a grounded `AgentDone` — the "second grounded-answer authority" 565 makes unrepresentable — now fails the build, the content-tier analog of 561's `interaction-surface` gate, for the one invariant with a clean structural form. Walks compiled bytecode (rename-proof), mirrors `AgentLoopServiceAuditTest`. **Proven to bite:** switching the max-iterations 4-arg ungrounded ctor to the 6-arg grounded ctor turned it red naming `AgentLoopService:581`; revert → green. **Honest scope:** pins the *attach seam* (no second authority), not the runtime property "every answer with hits IS grounded" (that stays `groundedDone`'s logic + the live check). The other two invariants stay discipline by design — status-tone's gate is genuinely infeasible (status-coloring is syntactically indistinguishable from legitimate semantic colour; verified the claimed `RetrospectivePanel` leak was a subagent hallucination — it already routes through `toneAccent(outcomeToTone(...))`), and run-renderers' Lit `html` templates aren't JSX so an AST gate buys ~nothing over the existing grep early-warning. Verified: `:modules:app-agent:test` green.
